Marathon Petroleum Corp. (NYSE&#58; MPC) today reported a net loss of $242 million, or $(0.37) per diluted share, for the first quarter of 2021, compared with a net loss of $9.2 billion, or $(14.25) per diluted share, for the first quarter of 2020.   </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted net loss was $132 million, or $(0.20) per diluted share, for the first quarter of 2021, compared with an adjusted net loss of $106 million, or $(0.16) per diluted share, for the first quarter of 2020.  First-quarter 2021 and first-quarter 2020 results include pre-tax charges of $70 million and $12.4 billion, respectively, as shown in the accompanying release tables.</font></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_4"></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8220;During the first quarter, our industry continued to struggle with effects of the pandemic,&#34; said Michael J. Hennigan, president and chief executive officer. &#34;With the COVID-19 vaccination roll-out, we are beginning to see increases in global mobility and demand for transportation fuels. For the first time since the pandemic began our Refining and Marketing business generated positive adjusted EBITDA. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#34;We have also continued the strategic effort to reposition our company for long term success, both through the pending Speedway sale and our investments in renewables projects. The Speedway transaction is close to completion, and we reiterate our commitment to use proceeds from this transaction to strengthen the balance sheet and return capital to shareholders. Our Board of Directors approved the conversion of the Martinez refinery, and we are excited that, once permitting, engineering, and implementation are complete, Martinez will be one of the largest renewables facilities in the country.&#34; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">1</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_7"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Results from Operations</font></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_10"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">As previously announced, on Aug. 2, 2020, MPC entered into a definitive agreement to sell Speedway to 7-Eleven, Inc. for $21 billion in cash. Consistent with the reporting from prior quarters&#58; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font discontinued operations.</font><font style="color:#ee2724;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font &#38; Marketing segment.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">(a)</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:10.87pt">As of August 2, 2020, MPC ceased recording depreciation and amortization for Speedway. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:3pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font><br></font></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_16"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Refining &#38; Marketing (R&#38;M)</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">As discussed above, R&#38;M segment results include the results of the direct dealer business. Prior periods reflect this change in segment presentation. </font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">R&#38;M segment loss from operations was $598 million in the first quarter of 2021, compared with a loss of $497 million for the first quarter of 2020. </font><font style="color:#ee2724;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment adjusted EBITDA was $23 million in the first quarter of 2021, versus $305 million for the first quarter of 2020. Segment adjusted EBITDA excludes refining planned turnaround costs, which totaled $112 million in the first quarter of 2021 and $329 million in the first quarter of 2020.  First-quarter 2021 segment adjusted EBITDA also excludes winter storm effects of $31 million. The decrease in R&#38;M earnings was primarily due to lower throughput and narrower crude differentials, partially offset by reduced operating costs.  </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">R&#38;M margin was $10.16 per barrel for the first quarter of 2021, versus $11.86 for the first quarter of 2020. Crude capacity utilization was 83%, resulting in total throughput of 2.6 million barrels per day. Clean product yield was 85%. </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">3</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_19"></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Midstream</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Midstream segment income from operations, which primarily reflects the results of MPLX LP (NYSE&#58; MPLX), was $972 million in the first quarter of 2021, compared with $905 million for the first quarter of 2020. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Segment adjusted EBITDA was $1.3 billion in the first quarter of 2021, versus $1.3 billion for the first quarter of 2020.  First-quarter 2021 segment adjusted EBITDA excludes winter storm effects of $16 million.  Results for the quarter benefited from lower operating expenses and were offset by lower gathered and processed volumes. </font></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_22"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Corporate and Items Not Allocated</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Corporate expenses totaled $157 million in the first quarter of 2021, compared with $233 million in the first quarter of 2020. </font><font style="color:#ee2724;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the first quarter of 2020, items not allocated to segments included net charges of $12.3 billion.  </font></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_25"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Speedway </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:6pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The results of Speedway are required to be reported separately as discontinued operations. MPC ceased recording depreciation and amortization (D&#38;A) for Speedway in August 2020. Therefore, first-quarter 2021 results reflect no D&#38;A, as compared to $99 million of D&#38;A in first-quarter 2020. Results for all periods presented also exclude any allocation of corporate costs to Speedway. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Speedway income from operations was $330 million in the first quarter of 2021, compared with $400 million for the first quarter of 2020. Speedway&#8217;s adjusted EBITDA was $332 million in the first quarter of 2021, versus $499 million for the first quarter of 2020. First-quarter 2021 results reflect lower fuel margins and lower fuel volumes, partially offset by higher merchandise sales compared to the prior year.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Speedway fuel margin was 25.67 cents per gallon in the first quarter of 2021, versus 35.40 cents per gallon in the first quarter of 2020. Same-store merchandise sales increased by 7.0% year-over-year and Speedway same-store gasoline sales volume decreased by 12.3% year-over-year, reflecting the impacts of the pandemic.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Discontinued operations for the first quarter of 2021 included $23 million of costs related to the separation of Speedway, compared with the first quarter of 2020 which included a $35 million lower of cost or market (LCM) inventory charge and $27 million of costs related to the Speedway separation.</font></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_28"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Financial Position and Liquidity </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">As of March 31, 2021, the company had $734 million in cash and cash equivalents (excluding MPLX&#8217;s cash and cash equivalents of $24 million), $1.3 billion outstanding under its $5 billion five-year bank revolving credit facility, no borrowings outstanding under its $1 billion 364-day bank revolving credit facility, and no borrowings outstanding under its $750 million trade receivables securitization facility. The company had $1.7 billion of outstanding commercial paper borrowings as of March 31, 2021. MPC does not intend to have outstanding commercial paper borrowings in excess of available capacity under its bank revolving credit facilities. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company repaid the $1.0 billion of 5.125% senior notes that matured in March 2021.</font></div><div id="i725f5652d1674cdbad1f0a6692d41db3_31"></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Strategic and Operations Update</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The company is close to completion on the $21 billion sale of Speedway to 7-Eleven and expects to use proceeds from the sale to strengthen the balance sheet and return capital to shareholders.&#160; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">MPC&#8217;s Board of Directors approved the conversion of the Martinez, California facility to a renewable diesel plant. The Martinez facility is expected to produce 17,000 barrels per day of renewable diesel by </font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">4</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt;text-align:right"><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:72pt;width:100%"><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">the second half of 2022, with pretreatment capabilities coming online in 2023. The facility is expected to be capable of producing 48,000 barrels per day by the end of 2023. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Consistent with MPC's midstream strategy of developing long-haul pipelines and other logistics solutions, several projects advanced during the quarter, including the Wink to Webster crude oil pipeline, the Whistler natural gas pipeline, and the reversal of the Capline crude pipeline. Each of these projects includes minimum volume commitments from customers.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt"><font The company operates the nation&#8217;s largest refining system. MPC&#8217;s marketing system includes branded locations across the United States, including Marathon brand retail outlets. Speedway LLC, an MPC subsidiary, owns and operates retail convenience stores across the United States. MPC also owns the general partner and majority limited partner interest in MPLX LP, a midstream company that owns and operates gathering, processing, and fractionation assets, as well as crude oil and light product transportation and logistics infrastructure. We believe these non-GAAP financial measures are useful to investors and analysts to assess our ongoing financial performance because, when reconciled to their most comparable GAAP financial measures, they provide improved comparability between periods through the exclusion of certain items that we believe are not indicative of our core operating performance and that may obscure our underlying business results and trends. We have excluded these items because we believe that they are not indicative of our core operating performance and that their exclusion results in an important measure of our ongoing financial Segment Adjusted EBITDA</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:3pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted EBITDA and Segment Adjusted EBITDA represent earnings before net interest and other financial costs, income taxes, depreciation and amortization expense as well as adjustments to exclude refining turnaround costs, items not allocated to segment results and other items shown in the table below. We believe these non-GAAP financial measures are useful to investors and analysts to analyze and compare our operating performance between periods by excluding items that do not reflect the core operating results of our business or in the case of turnarounds, which provide benefits over multiple years. We also believe that excluding turnaround costs from this metric is useful for comparability to other companies as certain of our competitors defer these costs and amortize them between turnarounds. Adjusted EBITDA and Segment Adjusted EBITDA should not be considered as a substitute for, or superior to segment income (loss) from operations, net income attributable to MPC, income before income taxes, cash flows from operating activities or any other measure of financial performance presented in accordance with GAAP. Adjusted EBITDA and Segment Adjusted EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures reported by other companies.</font></div><div
